# Apify Professional Services

Premium, customized professional services for web scraping and automation projects.

[Contact sales](/contact-sales/custom-web-scraper)

Trusted by

Professional services

## Let us build it for you

You'll love working with Apify

Our team will help you get data from any website, providing you with a tailor-made solution that drives your business forward. Our expertise spans customers from 100+ countries and a decade of scraping.

Migration made easy

Whether you already have code hosted externally or just want to switch to Apify from another data extraction provider, we can migrate your project and ensure that your code is fully compatible with our platform.

Enterprise-level SLA

The Service Level Agreement (SLA) is insurance for your project, with an agreement on expected deliverables, automated monitoring, response times for issues, and a customized maintenance package.

Stable, dedicated delivery team

You will be assigned a Technical Project Manager, Lead Engineer, and Account Manager. You can rely on them to be consistent and reliable, so youâ€™ll always be dealing with the same friendly faces who know your project inside out.

Monitoring and maintenance

Our automated monitoring system checks for data quality, completion, and delivery confirmation, while the maintenance package means that our team will fix issues quickly.

Flexible integrations

Apify can be easily plugged into your existing workflows, using ready-made integrations with Zapier, Make, Google, and many other services. We can also build a custom integration for your specific data pipeline.

Closer to your time zone

Apify's HQ is in the EU, so we're perfectly placed to help both US and EU clients. This means we're here for you during your working hours, making it easier to get support and updates right when you need them.

Access to our legal experts

Apify believes in ethical web scraping and our legal team can advise you on when you should be concerned about terms of service or international regulations, especially the GDPR in the European Union.

Customer Stories

## See how we've helped other companies

[How Groupon finds and reaches new merchants thanks to web data collection](https://blog.apify.com/groupon-reaches-new-merchants-with-web-data-collection/)[How Intercom uses Apify to feed web data to its AI chatbot for customer support](https://blog.apify.com/intercom-customer-support-ai-chatbot-web-scraping/)[How web scraping, AI, and the European Commission have come together to fight fake discounts in Europe](https://blog.apify.com/how-web-scraping-ai-and-the-eu-have-come-together-to-sweep-away-fake-discounts-in-europe/)

[Find your use case in our customer success stories](/success-stories)

## Let's discuss your project

We can build a complete end-to-end solution or help you migrate your existing scrapers to Apify.

[Contact sales](/contact-sales/custom-web-scraper)

## Want to monitor, scale, and optimize? Relax, we've got you covered.

We will carry out proactive monitoring and maintenance of your web scraping and automation tasks. And your SLA will guarantee that we communicate issues and begin working on a solution within a predetermined time. We are usually able to report and fix issues very quickly.

4,000+Customers worldwide

4 B+Web pages crawled monthly

100+Team of talented Apifiers

Why Apify?

## Built for mission-critical projects

No vendor lock-in

Apify is an open platform, and you own the code, so there's no vendor lock-in. We'll gladly help you to onboard your engineering team so you can retain full control of your solutions.

World-class Apify experts

Our team of experienced web scraping professionals can onboard your team and host workshops. We've been scraping for a long time and we love to share our knowledge.

Great documentation and onboarding

We'll help you understand how to get the most out of the Apify platform and provide in-depth documentation for your custom solution that your team can learn from and build on.

Maximum privacy

You will get an NDA and details of your projects and data will never be shared with third parties. You will always have complete control over your datasets and solutions.

Extremely scalable

The Apify platform can easily scale to hundreds of millions of web pages per month and terabytes of data. Our [new request queue](https://blog.apify.com/new-apify-request-queue/) comfortably handles up to 500,000 API requests every minute.

SOC 2 compliance in progress

We are actively working towards SOC 2 certification to make sure that we meet all essential security standards by end-2024. Until then, we're more than happy to complete your security questionnaires.

## How we deliver value to our clients

[Actor bundles](https://blog.apify.com/apify-power-actors/) are a great example of the kind of projects we regularly complete for enterprise clients. Here's a diagram of a solution we prepared for the European Commission. The AI-powered Actor scrapes data from the product URLs of European online stores to monitor their pricing strategies. If a store is not complying with regulations, the authority is automatically notified. As of June 2024, Apify has helped the EU monitor more than 42,000 products from 740 e-retailers.

## Frequently asked questions

### What does the SLA mean for my project?

A service-level agreement (SLA) is essential to make sure both you and Apify are on the same page in terms of standards and service. By signing a service level agreement, we'll have a clearly documented method of working through our mutual expectations. For example, SLAs guarantee that we communicate discovered issues within a predetermined time, and we also guarantee to begin working on the solution within a set number of days or hours.

### Do you support websites in different languages?

Yes, we can extract data and automate workflows on websites in any language. We can also extract data from mobile apps.

### Can we migrate the solution to our own infrastructure?

You will own the intellectual property rights to the custom delivered software. The solutions are typically built using the open-source Apify SDK and other open-source libraries and tools, which can run on any computer outside the Apify platform. So it is definitely possible to migrate your solutions from the Apify platform to your own infrastructure.

### How much will it cost?

The exact pricing depends on a number of factors, such as the number and complexity of target websites, amount of blocking, data volumes, SLA parameters, etc. Simply send us the details of your project and our team will provide you with an estimate.   
  
Please note that our fully managed Enterprise solutions start at $2,000 per month. For more affordable ways to order custom solutions, please check out [Apify Partners](https://apify.com/partners/freelancers).

### Can you maintain an existing web scraping project for us?

Yes. We are also able to help with the migration of existing scrapers to Apify and can manage your web scraping infrastructure.

### What does the typical process look like?

After submitting your request, a member of our team will contact you to discuss your project in more detail. The next step is that we will prepare a proposal for you detailing all the deliverables, timeline and associated costs. After you approve the proposal, we will prepare an agreement to finalize the details. Once signed, development of your solution will start. The solution will be delivered in the form of one or more [Actors](https://apify.com/actors) on the Apify platform.

### Is web scraping legal?

Web scraping is legal if you scrape data publicly available on the internet. However, some kinds of data are protected by international regulations, such as personal data, intellectual property, or confidential data. You can learn more in our blog post about the [legality of web scraping.](https://blog.apify.com/is-web-scraping-legal/)   
  
But rest assured that our legal experts will analyze your project and will provide you with guidance. Please note that Apify is a proponent of not only legal, but also ethical scraping that doesn't overburden the target sites.

Get in touch and we'll discuss your project.

# About Apify

Weâ€™re building the worldâ€™s best cloud platform for developing and running web scraping solutions.

## Founded in 2015

Apify was launched by Jan ÄŒurn and Jakub Balada in 2015 from the Y Combinator Fellowship in Mountain View, California. The original idea was to make it easy for developers to build flexible and scalable web crawlers simply using front-end JavaScript, thanks to the back-then new headless browser technology.

## Built with â¤ï¸ and ðŸº in Prague

In 2016, the team moved back to the Czech Republic, raised a seed investment, and started building a company around its product. Soon it became obvious that customersâ€™ use cases need more than a simple JavaScript crawler, so we committed to building the most flexible full-stack platform for web scraping and browser automation.

## Our mission

We make the web more programmable, to let people automate mundane tasks on the web and spend their time on things that matter. We strive to keep the web open as a public good and a basic right for everyone, regardless of the way you want to use it, as its creators intended.

4,000+Customers worldwide

4 B+Web pages crawled monthly

3,000+Ready-made Actors in Store

# Customer stories

Get inspired by these awesome projects. Find out how Apify can make your work more efficient, profitable, useful, and add value to everything you do.

## Helping communities, workplaces, and families

Explore how web scraping fosters bonds in families and communities by uncovering lost loved ones by scraping social media, helps an IT company with their lunch planning, and aids migrant integration by collecting dialect insights.

[**Fighting child traffickers with technology**  
Thorn is a non-profit organization dedicated to defending children against sexual abuse by collecting data to identify child exploitation.](/success-stories/fighting-child-traffickers-with-technology)[**Finding lost dogs and cats with scraping**  
Apify's cloud platform, web scraping tools, and crowdsourcing have even been used to reunite lost dogs (and cats!) with their humans.](/success-stories/the-lost-dog-app)[**How web scraping helps an IT company eat better**  
Don't know which restaurant to eat at during your lunch break? This clever IT company solved that problem by web scraping restaurant menus.](https://blog.apify.com/how-web-scraping-helps-an-it-company-eat-better/)[**How web scraping is bridging language barriers**  
Building a machine translation module for migrants and refugees faced a challenge that only web scraping could solve.](https://blog.apify.com/how-web-scraping-is-bridging-language-barriers-for-migrants-and-refugees-in-the-eu/)

## Powering AI with Data

Uncover the synergy of web scraping and AI in eradicating false discounts across Europe, witness how collaboration with Apify revolutionizes reuniting families through data-driven efforts, how a company uses our scrapers to power their chatbot, and unleash AI's prowess for enhanced SEO content.

[**Web scraping, AI, and the EU tackle fake discounts**  
Even if you didnâ€™t know it, before the COVID-19 pandemic, another plague was sweeping Europe, and itâ€™s still prevalent today: fake discounts.](https://blog.apify.com/how-web-scraping-ai-and-the-eu-have-come-together-to-sweep-away-fake-discounts-in-europe/)[**Web scraping and AI help to find missing children**  
Missing Children began with a Facebook page. With help from Boston University and Apify, the initiative is now reuniting families all over Egypt.](https://blog.apify.com/web-scraping-ai-missing-children/)[**How Intercom uses Apify to feed data to its AI chatbot**  
Fin, Intercomâ€™s new customer support AI chatbot, uses Apify's web crawling technology to extract data from customer websites and documentation.](https://blog.apify.com/intercom-customer-support-ai-chatbot-web-scraping/)[**Keyword research and content ideation tool**  
Topic is an AI-powered platform that analyzes existing top results in Google to surface valuable insights and enable teams to write better SEO content.](/success-stories/keyword-search-and-content-ideation-tool)

## Monitoring worldwide policy

Delve into the power of web scraping in tracking war crimes in Ukraine, gathering rainforest preservation policies, and curbing unlicensed online content.

[**Using web scraping to track down war crimes in Ukraine**  
How Mnemonic is using web scraping to collect social media data for use in international law, journalism, research, and memory preservation.](https://blog.apify.com/using-web-scraping-to-preserve-digital-memory-of-war-crimes-in-ukraine/)[**Helping to save the planet with scraped data**  
Omdena used Apify's tools to scrape and download thousands of policy documents and promote forest and landscape restoration in Latin America.](/success-stories/helping-the-planet-with-data)[**Illegal online content detector in Czechia**  
How web scraping helps content publishers reduce losses by detecting unauthorized online copies of books and audiovisual content.](/success-stories/illegal-content-detector)[**Monitoring the use of copyrighted music**  
See how Deecoob utilize web scraping to fuel their music royalty and licensing platform, MESLIS.](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=CQnRcaEATho)

## Providing essential real estate and map data

Dive into mapping out a 15-minute city, exploring Massachusetts property tax, scraping Czech Republic's apartment listings, and crafting a real estate aggregator.

[**How to build a 15-minute city with map data**  
Find out how extracting quantitative data from Google Maps can help us understand and suggest improvements in the urban environment.](https://blog.apify.com/google-maps-data-15-minute-city/)[**Scraping American real estate market for research**  
The challenges of collecting data on the American real estate market for tax research and how Apify's web scraper simplified the whole process.](/success-stories/scrape-americas-real-estate-tax-research)[**Analyzing holiday home prices with web scraping**  
How two students scraped real estate listings to examine Czech Republic's holiday home cost surge, COVID-19 effects, and wage-price disparity.](/success-stories/scrape-czech-holiday-home-research)[**Real estate aggregator site using web scraping**  
In one of our earliest success stories, a real estate aggregator scraped listings from the 23 largest websites offering properties for sale and rent.](/success-stories/real-estate-aggregator)

## Scraping price data and monitoring for changes

Explore cost-effective web scraping success, Apify's e-commerce price monitoring solutions, and our revealing analysis of inflated pricing tactics.

[**Moving from Scrapy saved 90% in web scraping costs**  
How Daltix managed to make a big move from Scrapy to Apify and from Python to JavaScript and what the payoffs were.](success-stories/daltix-analytics-scrapy-python-to-apify)[**Retailer price monitoring with web scraping**  
A leading manufacturer used Apify to monitor product prices on e-commerce websites to ensure they are never priced lower than the agreed minimum.](success-stories/retailer-price-monitoring)[**Black Friday fake discount analysis**  
Apify regularly conducts extensive scraping of prices to determine the average and real Black Friday discount at the largest Czech online stores.](https://blog.apify.com/last-unregulated-black-friday-in-czechia-fewer-discounts-claimed/)

## Revolutionizing job data extraction

From success with automated Apify Actors in job searching for mothers and how Czechitas uses web scraping to make it easier for women to apply for job positions.

[**Scraping part-time job offers for working moms**  
It can be especially difficult for women who have children to find part-time jobs when they want to return to the workplace. Apify Actors made it easy.](/success-stories/scraping-job-offers-for-moms)[**Bringing IT opportunities closer to women**  
See how Czechitas teamed up with Apify to collect and analyze posted job advertisements for junior IT positions all over the country in various cities.](/success-stories/women-it-opportunity)

## Elevating data analysis with web scraping

Dive into the world of data-driven journalism, the coverage of terrorism in the media, a client's strategic edge through competitor analysis, seamless data extraction transforming customer success, and the creation of an SEO audit tool.

[**Terror or clickbait? How the media covers terrorism**  
Students at the Czechitas Digital Academy created an interactive dashboard demonstrating how the media covers terrorism.](/success-stories/terror-or-clickbait)[**Automated competitive intelligence**  
How an educational company extracted data about courses from their competitor and own websites on a weekly basis.](/success-stories/automated-competitive-intelligence)[**Scaling up AI-powered content agency**  
How a B2B content analysis agency used the Apify API to pass data into their content intelligence NoSQL database.](/success-stories/content-data-extraction-content-agency)[**Web scraping to identify on-page SEO issues**  
Finding on-page SEO issues can be tricky. Read about how Apify helped develop an SEO audit tool for their customers.](/success-stories/seo-audit-tool)

## Empowering user stories

Embrace the versatility of Apify tools like our users that create custom RSS feeds, scrape Amazon search results, automate concert notifications, and earn passive income.

[**RSS feed from any website**  
Want to keep tabs on a website that doesn't provide an RSS feed? This guide shows you how you can use an Apify crawler to make your own.](https://www.mozzafiller.com/posts/create-an-rss-feed-from-any-website-using-apify)[**Scraping Amazon**  
Shows you how a request queue can drill down for product details and provides extensively commented code to guide you through the process.](https://www.scaleleap.com/zine/how-to-scrape-amazon/)[**Personalised concert tips**  
Great guide to using Apify and Songkick to get automatically notified about concerts and gigs by artists similar to your favorites.](https://www.mozzafiller.com/posts/personalised-concert-recommendations-using-songkick-and-apify-actors)[**Earning from scrapers**  
Discover how one of our first freelance devs went on to earn regular monthly passive income from letting others use his Actors on the Apify platform.](/success-stories/paid-actor-journey-apify-freelancer-tugkan)

## Finding leads all across the web

See how companies utilized automated web data extraction to find and filter contacts and potential business partners.

[**Groupon reaches new merchants** How did Groupon create a rich lead generation database? In a word: Apify.](https://blog.apify.com/groupon-reaches-new-merchants-with-web-data-collection/)[**Scaling email marketing and lead generation with itrinity and Apify**  
How itrinity uses Apify to take its email verification and outreach strategies to another level.](https://blog.apify.com/scale-email-marketing-and-lead-generation/)

# Apify for startups

Apify believes in encouraging startups to grow by making use of online data at scale. So we're giving a special 30% discount on our Scale plan to startups.

Apply now

## Start scraping right away

Grow your startup with the 4,000+ ready-made tools (Actors) available on [Apify Store](https://apify.com/store). Just search for an Actor to scrape specific website data and use it for [sentiment analysis](https://apify.com/use-cases/sentiment-analysis), [market research](https://apify.com/use-cases/market-research), [price comparison](https://apify.com/use-cases/price-comparison), [product development](https://apify.com/use-cases/product-development), and much [more](https://apify.com/use-cases).

### [Website Content Crawlerapify/website-content-crawlerCrawl websites and extract text content to feed AI models, LLM applications, vector databases, or RAG pipelines. The Actor supports rich formatting using Markdown, cleans the HTML, downloads files, and integrates well with ðŸ¦œðŸ”— LangChain, LlamaIndex, and the wider LLM ecosystem.Apify39.5k4.6/5](/apify/website-content-crawler)### [Instagram Scraperapify/instagram-scraperScrape and download Instagram posts, profiles, places, hashtags, photos, and comments. Get data from Instagram using one or more Instagram URLs or search queries. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs or integrate with other tools.Apify78.7k4.3/5](/apify/instagram-scraper)### [Web Scraperapify/web-scraperCrawls arbitrary websites using the Chrome browser and extracts structured data from web pages using a provided JavaScript function. The Actor supports both recursive crawling and lists of URLs, and automatically manages concurrency for maximum performance.Apify77.6k4.5/5](/apify/web-scraper)### [Google Maps Scrapercompass/crawler-google-placesExtract data from thousands of Google Maps locations and businesses. Get Google Maps data including reviews, reviewer details, images, contact info, opening hours, location, prices & more. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs, or integrate with other tools.Compass87.6k4.5/5](/compass/crawler-google-places)### [TikTok Scraperclockworks/tiktok-scraperExtract data from TikTok videos, hashtags, and users. Use URLs or search queries to scrape TikTok profiles, hashtags, posts, URLs, shares, followers, hearts, names, video, and music-related data. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs or integrate with other tools.Clockworks22.2k4.5/5](/clockworks/tiktok-scraper)### [Amazon Product Scraperjunglee/Amazon-crawlerUse this Amazon scraper to collect data based on URL and country from the Amazon website. Extract product information without using the Amazon API, including reviews, prices, descriptions, and Amazon Standard Identification Numbers (ASINs). Download data in various structured formats.Junglee8.1k4.5/5](/junglee/Amazon-crawler)

[Browse 4,000+ ready-made scrapers](https://apify.com/store)

## Are you a developer?

Use your own code and run it on the Apify platform to automate your workflow in the cloud and [integrate it](https://apify.com/integrations) with other services. The [Apify Docs](https://docs.apify.com/) have everything you need to get started.

[Start with PythonScrape single page with provided URL with HTTPX and extract data from page's HTML with Beautiful Soup.](/templates/python-start)[Start with JavaScriptScrape single page with provided URL with Axios and extract data from page's HTML with Cheerio.](/templates/js-start)[Start with TypeScriptScrape single page with provided URL with Axios and extract data from page's HTML with Cheerio.](/templates/ts-start)

[View more web scraping templates](/templates)

Connect to hundreds of apps right away using ready-made integrations, or set up your own with webhooks and our API.

## How do I sign up for the discount?

1

### Sign up for Apify

First, if you don't have an account with Apify yet, [sign up](https://console.apify.com/sign-up) with your **company email**.

2

### Fill out the form

Fill out the form below. Please note that **discounts are only available for startups that meet criteria** described below in FAQs.

3

### Wait for Apifyâ€™s response

Our team will review your application. Give us time for this step! If we find your startup's use case compelling, we'll reach out to you with a discount coupon.

4

### Make the most of your discount!

You can apply the discount code in [your billing section](https://console.apify.com/billing/subscription) and extract data with a discounted Scale plan.

Fill out the form

## Frequently asked questions

### Who is eligible for the discount? 

Here are the requirements for us to consider giving you the startup discount:

  * Your startup is a **Software-as-a-Service company** or a different company where **Apify will play a critical role in your product or offering**.
  * You will **use Apify as part of your product or offering** , not for sales-related activities (such as lead generation) as long as the discount is applied.
  * Your startup has **raised less than USD 5 million in funding** , including Series A.
  * The project where you want to use Apify is **already live**.
  * You are **already using Apify using your company email** and know how you'll use the platform for your project. Note that all freemail applications will be automatically declined.
  * You agree to **use only your own Actors, Actors maintained by Apify, or community-maintained Actors that are either free or have a monthly fee**. Use of community-maintained Actors that are pay per result is not allowed for as long as the discount is applied.
  * You will subscribe to our **Scale plan for the whole duration of the discount**.
  * Your objectives and circumstances are aligned with our plans and initiatives. These plans can change at our discretion.



### Can I use the discount if Iâ€™m a solo founder?

The discount is also available to solo founders. We don't evaluate solo founders any differently, so please feel free to apply.

### Are there any restrictions associated with the discount?

By applying the discount code, you agree that you will not use community-managed Actors that are pay per result.   
  
Other types of Actors are acceptable, e.g. your own Actors, Actors maintained by Apify, or community-managed Actors that are free or have a monthly fee.   
  
Violating this policy may result in termination of the discount code and billing of your account using the original non-discounted pricing.

### How long will I be able to use my discount?

You can enjoy the discount for 6 months, with the possibility of an extension to 12 months if you really need it. You can request an extension up to 1 month before expiry.

### What level of support will I receive?

The Scale plan contains our chat support and 1 hour of technical training per quarter that will help you get the most value out of Apify.

### When will I know if the discount is approved? 

We typically reply within 2 weeks. We reply to all applicants unless they've unsubscribed from our email communication.

# Market research

Use web scraping to uncover deep insights from reviews, social media, comments, and forums. Find out what real customers are saying about you and your competitors.

[Browse tools](/store/categories/market-research)

## Get data from the web and learn more about your customers

Web scraping gives you the tools to gather data from product reviews, news articles, social media, and forums. Use that data to make informed decisions on product development, marketing strategies, pricing, and distribution.

## Competitor analysis and benchmarking

Monitor and analyze your competitors' websites, social media accounts, and pricing strategies. Use the extracted data to better understand their strengths and weaknesses, identify gaps in the market, and develop strategies to differentiate yourself from the competition. And if youâ€™re only starting out, benchmarking against industry leaders can provide valuable insights to improve your products, services, and marketing.

## Lead generation and sales prospecting

Use web scraping to collect contact email addresses and phone numbers, both from websites or online directories. This data can be used to build a database of potential customers, which can be plugged into targeted sales and marketing campaigns. Web scraping can also help you identify key decision-makers in target organizations, find suitable influencers, or recruit top candidates.

### [Contact Details Scrapervdrmota/contact-info-scraperFree email extractor and lead scraper to extract and download emails, phone numbers, Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn, and Instagram profiles from any website. ## Product and market trend analysis

Collect and analyze data on popular products, market trends, and customer preferences from sources such as e-commerce platforms, forums, and blogs. Use the information to identify emerging trends, understand consumer demands, and develop new products or services that cater to evolving market needs.

## Industry and regulatory compliance

Understand the regulatory landscape and industry-specific requirements that your business must safely navigate. Systematically extract data from government databases, industry associations, and online news sources to keep track of industry regulations, standards, and policies. Minimize the risks of non-compliance, such as fines, legal issues, and reputational damage.

## Frequently asked questions

### What is web scraping and how can it help me with market research?

If you were to do market research prices manually, you'd probably have to pay a lot of money (typically more than $15,000) for a custom industry report or collect data online yourself. Then you would need to put it into a structured database or even just an Excel spreadsheet. Web scraping does this job for you and creates datasets of structured data from the web pages that you point it to. Scraping is essential if you want to do market research at scale and it will save you an immense amount of time.

### Is it legal to scrape data for market research?

It is legal to scrape publicly available data such as product descriptions, prices, or ratings. On the other hand, certain types of data, such as personal data or copyrighted content, are under special legal protection and you should not scrape these without first making sure you follow the relevant laws and regulations. Read through our blog post on the [web scraping legality](https://blog.apify.com/is-web-scraping-legal/) to learn more about the law and extracting data from the web. Web scraping for market research is specfically permitted in the European Union by the [DSM directive](https://blog.apify.com/is-web-scraping-legal/#data-mining-in-the-european-union).

### I couldnâ€™t find a scraper for my specific website. Can I build it?

Knock yourself out! Our platform was built to host and run thousands of scrapers. You can customize a [universal Web Scraper](https://apify.com/store/scrapers/universal-web-scrapers) or start a new one with some of our [ready-made templates](https://apify.com/templates) in Python, JavaScript, or TypeScript. You can keep the scraper to yourself or make it public by adding it to Apify Store (and even make a [little cash](https://blog.apify.com/make-regular-passive-income-developing-web-automation-actors-b0392278d085/) out of it). You can also [integrate](https://apify.com/integrations) your scraper with other popular data processing services such as Keboola, Airbyte, or Zapier.

### I donâ€™t need to download scraped data. Is there an API I can use instead?

Yes, there is. You can have programmatic access to any scraper on the platform via Apify's web scraping API. It is organized around RESTful HTTP endpoints and can be accessed either by using Python or Node.js clients, or manually. This API will enable you to fetch results directly from any of your datasets. Check out the [Apify API reference docs](https://docs.apify.com/api/v2) for full details.

### I'm not a developer. Can you build a custom market research scraper for me?

Sure! We can build you a [custom web scraper](https://apify.com/contact-sales/custom-web-scraper) or, if you're searching for a more affordable solution, get an external developer to create the scraper for you via our [Apify freelancer program](https://apify.com/partners/freelancers).

### I donâ€™t need scrapers for market research, but I know somebody who does. Can I refer them?

Yes. Our affiliate program offers up to 50% recurring commission for its participants. You can check out the terms & conditions and sign up for Apify Affiliate [here](https://apify.com/partners/affiliate).

# Fast, reliable data for ChatGPT and LLMs

Extract text content from the web to feed your vector databases, fine-tune or train your large language models (LLMs) such as ChatGPT or LLaMA.

[Browse extractors for AI](https://apify.com/store/categories/ai)

POWERING THE WORLD'S TOP DATA-DRIVEN TEAMS

## Generative AI is powered by web scraping

Data is the fuel for AI, and web is the largest source of data ever created. Today's most popular language models like ChatGPT or LLaMA were all **trained on data scraped from the web.** Apify gives you the same superpowers and brings the vast amounts of data from the web to your fingertips.

Load vector databases

Extract documents from the web and load them to vector databases for querying and prompt generation.

Train new models

Extract text and images from the web to generate training datasets for your new AI models.

Fine-tune models

Use domain-specific data extracted from the web with the OpenAI fine-tuning API or other models.

## LangChain and LlamaIndex integration

Load scraped datasets directly into LangChain or LlamaIndex vector indexes. Build AI chatbots and other apps that query text data crawled from websites such as documentation, knowledge bases, blog posts, and other online sources.

## Frequently asked questions

### What is generative AI?

Generative AI is a type of deep learning model focused on generating text, images, audio, video, code, and other data types in response to text prompts. Examples of generative AI models are ChatGPT, MidJourney, and BARD.

### What is the difference between AI and generative AI?

AI is a field of computer science that aims to create intelligent machines or systems that can perform tasks that typically require human intelligence. Generative AI is a subfield of AI focused on creating systems capable of generating new content, such as images, text, music, or video.

### What are large language models?

Large language models, or LLMs, are a form of generative AI. They are typically transformer models that use deep learning methods to understand and generate text in a human-like fashion. Examples of LLMs are ChatGPT, LLaMA, LLaMDA, and BARD.

### What is data ingestion?

Data ingestion is the process of collecting, processing, and preparing data for analysis or machine learning. In the context of LLMs, data ingestion involves collecting text data ([web scraping](https://apify.com/web-scraping)), preprocessing it (cleaning, normalization, tokenization), and preparing it for training (feature engineering).

### Why use web scraping for AI?

[Web scraping](https://apify.com/web-scraping) allows you to collect reliable, up-to-date information that can be used to feed, fine-tune, or train large language models (LLMs) or provide context for prompts for ChatGPT. In return, the model will answer questions based on your or your customer's websites and content.

### What are vector databases?

Vector databases are designed to handle the unique structure of vector embeddings, which are dense vectors of numbers that represent text. They are used in machine learning to index vectors for easy search and retrieval by comparing values and finding those that are most similar to one another.

### What is LangChain?

LangChain is an open-source framework for developing applications powered by language models. It connects to the AI models you want to use and links them with outside sources. That means you can chain commands together so the AI model can know what it needs to do to produce the answers or perform the tasks you require.

### What is Pinecone?

Pinecone is a popular vector database that lets you provide long-term memory for high-performance AI applications. It is used for semantic search, similarity search for images and audio, recommendation systems, record matching, anomaly detection, and natural language processing.

### How do I train LLMs with scraped data?

  1. Data collection: use a tool like Apify's [Website Content Crawler](https://apify.com/apify/website-content-crawler) to scrape web data. Configure the crawler settings like start URLs, crawler type, HTML processing, and data cleaning to tailor the data to what you need.
  2. Data processing: clean and process the scraped data by removing unnecessary HTML elements, duplications, and transforming it into a usable format (e.g. JSON, CSV).
  3. Integration and training: integrate the cleaned and processed data with tools like LangChain or Pinecone and feed it into your LLM to fine-tune or train the model according to your specific requirements. Check out this full step-by-step tutorial on [how to collect data for LLMs with web scraping](https://blog.apify.com/webscraping-ai-data-for-llms).



### What is retrieval-augmented generation?

[RAG](https://blog.apify.com/what-is-retrieval-augmented-generation/) is an AI framework and technique used in natural language processing that combines elements of both retrieval-based and generation-based approaches to enhance the quality and relevance of generated text. It is used as a way to improve generative AI systems.

### Why use RAG for chatbots?

[RAG](https://blog.apify.com/what-is-retrieval-augmented-generation/) is a popular method for creating chatbots because it combines retrieval-based and generative-based models. Retrieval-based models search a database for the most relevant answer. Generative models create answers on the fly. The combination of these two capabilities makes RAG chatbots adaptable and mitigates hallucinations.

## Try Apify for free

...to get reliable data for LLMs quickly and easily.

# Apify Storage

Scalable and reliable cloud data storage designed for web scraping and automation workloads.

[View documentation](https://docs.apify.com/platform/storage)

Benefits

## Specialized storage from Apify

### Enterprise-grade reliability, performance, and scalability

Store a few records or a few hundred million, with the same low latency and high reliability. We use Amazon Web Services for the underlying data storage, giving you high availability and peace of mind.

### Low-cost storage for web scraping and crawling

Apify provides low-cost storage carefully designed for the large workloads typical of web scraping and crawling operations.

### Easy to use

Data can be viewed on the web, giving you a quick way to review and share it with other people. The Apify [API](https://docs.apify.com/api/v2) and [SDK](https://docs.apify.com/sdk/js/) makes it easy to integrate our storage into your apps.

Features

## Weâ€™ve got you covered

[**Dataset**  
Store results from your web scraping, crawling or data processing jobs into Apify datasets and export them to various formats like JSON, CSV, XML, RSS, Excel or HTML.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/storage/dataset)[**Request queue**  
Maintain a queue of URLs of web pages in order to recursively crawl websites, starting from initial URLs and adding new links as they are found while skipping duplicates.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/storage/request-queue)[**Key-value store**  
Store arbitrary data records along with their MIME content type. The records are accessible under a unique name and can be written and read at a rapid rate.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/storage/key-value-store)

## Get data today. Not in months.

Launch new products, analytics, and train your AI models faster than the competition thanks to ready-made Actors.

### [Website Content Crawlerapify/website-content-crawlerCrawl websites and extract text content to feed AI models, LLM applications, vector databases, or RAG pipelines. The Actor supports rich formatting using Markdown, cleans the HTML, downloads files, and integrates well with ðŸ¦œðŸ”— LangChain, LlamaIndex, and the wider LLM ecosystem.Apify39.5k4.6/5](/apify/website-content-crawler)### [Instagram Scraperapify/instagram-scraperScrape and download Instagram posts, profiles, places, hashtags, photos, and comments. Get data from Instagram using one or more Instagram URLs or search queries. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs or integrate with other tools.Apify78.7k4.3/5](/apify/instagram-scraper)### [TikTok Data Extractorclockworks/free-tiktok-scraperExtract data about videos, users, and channels based on hashtags or scrape full user profiles including posts, total likes, name, nickname, numbers of comments, shares, followers, following, and more.Clockworks22.5k4.7/5](/clockworks/free-tiktok-scraper)### [Facebook Posts Scraperapify/facebook-posts-scraperExtract data from hundreds of Facebook posts from one or multiple Facebook pages and profiles. Get post URL, post text, page or profile URL, timestamp, number of likes, shares, comments, and more. Download the data in JSON, CSV, and Excel and use it in apps, spreadsheets, and reports.Apify19.1k4.5/5](/apify/facebook-posts-scraper)### [Cheerio Scraperapify/cheerio-scraperCrawls websites using raw HTTP requests, parses the HTML with the Cheerio library, and extracts data from the pages using a Node.js code. Supports both recursive crawling and lists of URLs. This actor is a high-performance alternative to apify/web-scraper for websites that do not require JavaScript.Apify6.6k4.7/5](/apify/cheerio-scraper)### [Google Maps Extractorcompass/google-maps-extractorExtract data from hundreds of places fast. Scrape Google Maps by keyword, category, location, URLs & other filters. Get addresses, contact info, opening hours, popular times, prices, menus & more. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs, or integrate with other tools.Compass32.4k4.3/5](/compass/google-maps-extractor)

# Apify Actors

Actors are serverless cloud programs that automate tasks like web scraping, data processing, and AI agents. They are called Actors because, like human actors, they perform actions based on a script. They scale from simple tasks to complex workflows and integrate easily with APIs, databases, and AI models.

[Browse pre-built Actors](/store)[Read the Actor whitepaper ](https://whitepaper.actor/)

Benefits

## Run locally or in the cloud

###  Long-running serverless jobs

Apify Actors can perform time-consuming jobs that are longer than the lifespan of a single HTTP transaction.

[Read the docs](https://docs.apify.com/platform/actors)

### Publish and monetize Actors

Join hundreds of developers who share their Actors on Apify Store and earn money from coding.

[Go to Apify Store](/store)

### Auto-generated user interface

Actors can easily define a user interface for their input configuration. Take advantage of lower-level features and settings, or run Actors using our API.

[Learn about input schema](https://docs.apify.com/academy/deploying-your-code/input-schema)

### Keep your Actor running

You can run Actors as real-time APIs with Actor Standby mode. It lets you keep the Actor ready in the background, waiting for incoming HTTP requests, just like a real-time web server or standard API server.

[Learn more](https://docs.apify.com/platform/actors/development/programming-interface/standby)

Features

## Actors have you covered

[**Integrations**   
Integrate your Actors with other systems. Connect Apify actors and tasks with your favorite web apps and cloud services.](integrations)[**Proxy**   
Improve the performance of your web scrapers by smartly rotating datacenter and residential IP addresses.](proxy)[**Storage**   
Store data from your Actors in one of our Apify storages: key-value stores, datasets, or request queues.](storage)

## What else do Actors give you?

Host code anywhere

Edit your code on our platform, fetch from a Git repository, or push from your machine.

Docker support

Actors run inside Docker containers on Apify servers. Use a custom Dockerfile.

Ready for scale

Run as many Actors as you need. The Apify platform provisions the necessary resources.

Custom memory and CPU

Assign each Actor any RAM volume needed. CPU share is allocated automatically.

Command-line tool

Develop and test your Actors locally, push them to the Apify platform when you're ready.

Logging

View and download logs to debug your code and monitor performance on production.

## Apify open source fair share

Apify will support and reward every open-source project on Apify Store. Just turn your code into an Actor and choose your reward tier.

[Join the program](/partners/open-source-fair-share)

## What are Actors?

Actors are lightweight, containerized programs that take JSON inputs, execute tasks, and return structured outputs. Inspired by UNIX philosophy, they offer a simple, composable approach to automation, web scraping, and AI workflows in the cloud.

[Read the whitepaper ](https://whitepaper.actor/)

## Ready to build your first Actor?

[Start developing](/templates)

# Apify for universities

We hope to see future generations take advantage of the vast amount of data available online. Thatâ€™s why weâ€™re offering a 50% discount on our paid plans to students of accredited educational institutions.

Apply now

## Start scraping right away

There are hundreds of ready-made tools (Actors) available on [Apify Store](https://apify.com/store). You can search for an Actor that scrapes specific website data needed for your research or use [universal web scrapers](https://apify.com/store/scrapers/universal-web-scrapers) that require some CSS knowledge.

### [Instagram Scraperapify/instagram-scraperScrape and download Instagram posts, profiles, places, hashtags, photos, and comments. Get data from Instagram using one or more Instagram URLs or search queries. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs or integrate with other tools.Apify78.7k4.3/5](/apify/instagram-scraper)### [Web Scraperapify/web-scraperCrawls arbitrary websites using the Chrome browser and extracts structured data from web pages using a provided JavaScript function. The Actor supports both recursive crawling and lists of URLs, and automatically manages concurrency for maximum performance.Apify77.6k4.5/5](/apify/web-scraper)### [Google Maps Scrapercompass/crawler-google-placesExtract data from thousands of Google Maps locations and businesses. Get Google Maps data including reviews, reviewer details, images, contact info, opening hours, location, prices & more. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs, or integrate with other tools.Compass87.6k4.5/5](/compass/crawler-google-places)### [TikTok Scraperclockworks/tiktok-scraperExtract data from TikTok videos, hashtags, and users. Use URLs or search queries to scrape TikTok profiles, hashtags, posts, URLs, shares, followers, hearts, names, video, and music-related data. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs or integrate with other tools.Clockworks22.2k4.5/5](/clockworks/tiktok-scraper)### [Amazon Product Scraperjunglee/Amazon-crawlerUse this Amazon scraper to collect data based on URL and country from the Amazon website. Extract product information without using the Amazon API, including reviews, prices, descriptions, and Amazon Standard Identification Numbers (ASINs). Download data in various structured formats.Junglee8.1k4.5/5](/junglee/Amazon-crawler)### [Twitter Scraperquacker/twitter-scraperScrape tweets from any Twitter user profile. Top Twitter API alternative to scrape Twitter hashtags, threads, replies, followers, images, videos, statistics, and Twitter history. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs or integrate with other tools.Quacker31.6k4.3/5](/quacker/twitter-scraper)

[Browse 2,000+ ready-made scrapers](https://apify.com/store)

## Are you a developer?

You can also use your own code and run it on our platform to automate your workflow in the cloud and [integrate it](https://apify.com/integrations) with other services. Get started with building Actors for our platform at [Apify Docs](https://docs.apify.com/).

[Start with PythonScrape single page with provided URL with HTTPX and extract data from page's HTML with Beautiful Soup.](/templates/python-start)[Start with JavaScriptScrape single page with provided URL with Axios and extract data from page's HTML with Cheerio.](/templates/js-start)[Start with TypeScriptScrape single page with provided URL with Axios and extract data from page's HTML with Cheerio.](/templates/ts-start)

## Apply data to your field

Data extracted with Apify web scrapers can be used in a wide range of research and industries. For instance, Apifyâ€™s Google Maps Scraper has been used to [map bakeries in Paris](https://blog.apify.com/french-data-researcher-playing-with-google-maps-to-scrape-all-bakeries-in-paris/) and [calculate the walkability of a city](https://blog.apify.com/google-maps-data-15-minute-city/).

[How a university researcher studies TikTok user behavior with web scrapingRead more](https://blog.apify.com/tiktok-user-behavior-with-apify/)[How to build a 15-minute city: a question answered by map dataRead more](https://blog.apify.com/google-maps-data-15-minute-city/)[Scraping Paris bakeries using Google Maps APIRead more](https://blog.apify.com/french-data-researcher-playing-with-google-maps-to-scrape-all-bakeries-in-paris/)

[Read customer stories](https://blog.apify.com/tag/case-studies/)

## How do I sign up for the discount?

1

### Fill out the form

First, create an Apify account with your university email and then fill out the form on [this page](https://apify.com/resources/universities#get-your-discount-now). Note that you are only eligible for a discount for one semester if it concerns a university project such as a thesis or diploma research.

2

### Wait for Apifyâ€™s response

If we think your use case is relevant to your studies, we will get back to you. We might even jump on a call to fill in any gaps.

3

### Make the most of your discount!

After deciding on the terms of your platform usage, we will modify your account so that you can extract data for your project at a reduced cost.

4

### Mention Apify in your publications

We would be delighted if you would consider referencing Apify in your research papers and online publications. This will help your colleagues and peers discover how web scraping can be used to gather data.

Fill out the form

We provide data to leading academic institutions

## Frequently asked questions

### Can I use the discount if Iâ€™m a lecturer?

The Apify for Universities discount is not limited to students and is applicable to any researcher with an edu e-mail address.

### Can I also use an ISIC card to verify my student status?

Your university e-mail should be enough to verify your student status, but in case you don't have access to it or prefer communication via your regular e-mail address, an ISIC card will suffice.

### How long will I be able to use my discount?

You will be able to use your discount for as long as you're working on your project, with one semester (four months) being the maximum.

### What level of support will I recieve?

The level of support depends on [the plan](https://apify.com/pricing) to which you apply your discount. For instance, with the Starter plan, you'll get e-mail support from Apify engineers.

### Can I get a discount if I'm still in high school?

If you're a high school (or secondary school) student, you're also eligible for an education discount. Just make sure to put your high school in the _University name_ field. Note that we will contact you to verify your student status.

# Apify integrations

Connect Apify Actors and tasks with your favorite web apps and cloud services, receive automatic email notifications, and bring your workflow automation to a whole new level.

#### Programming

##### [APIConnect to virtually any other cloud or local service using a RESTful API. Control almost every aspect of the Apify platform.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/api)##### [WebhooksConfigure the Apify platform to carry out an action when a system event occurs â€“ e.g., get a notification whenever an Actor run finishes.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/webhooks)##### [GitHubConnect Apify to your GitHub account and automatically create a new issue in your repository whenever an Actor run fails.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/github)##### [GitImport code from your GitHub, GitLab or Bitbucket repository when creating a new Apify Actor.](https://docs.apify.com/actors/development/source-code#git-repository)

#### Actor-to-Actor

##### [Actor-to-ActorAutomate your workflow by connecting the output of one Apify Actor with the input of another.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/actors)

#### Workflow & notification

##### [ZapierConnect Apify with 6,000+ apps via Zapier and automatically move data between them, including key-value stores and datasets.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/zapier)##### [MakeRun Apify Actors, monitor their statuses, and receive Actor results directly within your Make scenarios.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/make)##### [TelegramIntegrate your Apify Actors with Telegram through Zapier and get instant updates on your Actor runs.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/telegram)##### [SlackRun Apify web scraping tools as a team and streamline your automation workflows by centralizing them in Slack.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/slack)##### [GmailSend run information, dataset files, and output notifications to any e-mail address by integrating your Gmail account with Apify.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/gmail)##### [AsanaAutomate your web scraping workflow and create a new Asana task whenever an Actor run fails.](https://asana.com/apps/apify)##### [SIGNL4Send automated mobile alerts regarding changes on websites or critical errors, so that responsible users are swiftly notified.](https://www.signl4.com/blog/portfolio_item/apify/)

#### Data storage

##### [AirbyteConsolidate your data in your databases and plug results from Actors into your ETL pipelines easily.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/airbyte)##### [KeboolaAutomate anything from data extraction to predictions. Plug results from web scraping tools into your data processing pipelines.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/keboola)##### [Google DriveSign in via your Google account and upload dataset files to a Google Drive folder whenever a run succeeds.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/drive)##### [HevoReplicate data from your Apify account to a Destination database or data warehouse using Hevo Pipelines.](https://docs.hevodata.com/sources/engg-analytics/apify/)

#### AI

##### [LangChainRun Actors from LangChain and load their results into vector databases, ChatGPT, and other LLMs.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/langchain)##### [LlamaIndexUse Apify's data loaders to bring data from Actors and datasets to the open-source repository, LlamaHub.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/llama)##### [FlowiseAIIntegrate Apify with the open-source UI visual tool to build your customized LLM flow using LangChainJS.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/flowise)##### [PineconeSimplify your data operations by pushing selected fields from your Apify Actor directly into any Pinecone index.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/pinecone)##### [HaystackExtract data using Apify Actors, convert it into Haystack Documents, and perform advanced AI tasks.](https://docs.apify.com/platform/integrations/haystack)##### [MCPUse Apify Actors from your AI agents and workflows using Antrophic's Model Context Protocol (MCP).](/apify/actors-mcp-server)

## Integration Actors

Utility Actors that help import or export data between the Apify platform and third party systems.

### [Dataset Image Downloader & Uploaderlukaskrivka/images-download-uploadDownload image files from image URLs in your datasets and save them to a Zip file, Key-Value store, or directly your AWS S3 bucket.LukÃ¡Å¡ KÅ™ivka631](/lukaskrivka/images-download-upload)### [PDF Text Extractorjirimoravcik/pdf-text-extractorPDF Text Extractor allows you to extract text from PDF files. It also supports chunking of the text to prepare the data for usage with large language models.JiÅ™Ã­ MoravÄÃ­k4925.0/5](/jirimoravcik/pdf-text-extractor)### [API / JSON scraperpocesar/json-downloaderScrape any API / JSON URLs directly to the dataset, and return them in CSV, XML, HTML, or Excel formats. Transform and filter the output. Enables you to follow pagination recursively from the payload without the need to visit the HTML page.Paulo Cesar462](/pocesar/json-downloader)### [Send Emailapify/send-mailThe actor automatically sends an email to a specific address. This actor is useful for notifications and reporting. With only 3 lines of JavaScript code, you'll be on top of your scraping actors and never miss important results or issues.Apify2.7k4.7/5](/apify/send-mail)### [Download Images From Datasetzuzka/download-images-from-datasetDownload actual pictures from scraped dataset based on the image urls. The actor creates a zip file for you to download with one click.Zuzka PelechovÃ¡249](/zuzka/download-images-from-dataset)### [Merge, Dedup & Transform Datasetslukaskrivka/dedup-datasetsThe ultimate dataset processor. Extremely fast merging, deduplications & transformations all in a single run.LukÃ¡Å¡ KÅ™ivka4k](/lukaskrivka/dedup-datasets)

# Use cases

Learn how web scraping and browser automation with Apify can help grow your business.

[**Data for generative AI** Feed your vector databases and train your LLMs with data extracted from the web.](data-for-generative-ai)[**Lead generation** Find new potential customers and collect data about them at scale.](/use-cases/lead-generation)[**Machine learning** Generate large-scale datasets from the web for the training of your artificial intelligence models.](/use-cases/machine-learning)[**Market research** Monitor your online competitors and automatically react to changes in their prices.](/use-cases/market-research)[**Price comparison** Monitor your online competitors and automatically react to changes in their prices.](/use-cases/price-comparison )[**Product development** Build new products and services on top of existing web apps and data sources.](/use-cases/product-development)[**Product matching AI** Merge datasets of identical products with our all-in-one product-matching RPA.](product-matching-ai)[**RPA â€“ Robotic Process Automation** Monitor your online competitors and automatically react to changes in their prices.](/use-cases/rpa)[**Sentiment analysis** Supply your sentiment analysis projects with real-time web data no matter whether itâ€™s tweets, comments, product reviews, or news articles.](/use-cases/sentiment-analysis)[**Universal web scrapers** Save development time and start your web scraping project with ready-to-use boilerplate code.](store/scrapers/universal-web-scrapers)[**AI chatbot** Convert your website, blog, or FAQ into a chatbot-ready format.](use-cases/ai-chatbot)[**AI web data monitoring** Gather, process, and analyze web data to stay ahead in your industry.](/use-cases/ai-monitoring)

# Apify open source fair share

Apify will support and reward every open-source project on Apify Store. Just turn your code into an Actor and choose your reward tier.

[Join the program](https://apify.firstpromoter.com/signup/28997)

## Reward tiers

Passive tier

Get monthly payouts via your GitHub Sponsor button. No other action needed.

Maintainer tier

Register with Apify and claim ownership of the Actor to get usage insights.

Active developer tier

Optimize the Actor and maximize your income with a competitive advantage.

## Passive tier

We'll send a commission for every customer your open-source project brings to the Apify platform. You get **10% in their first 3 months** and then **20% commission in the following months** for as long as they remain our customers, up to $2,500 per customer. Note that this tier gives you **no insights into traffic.**

## Maintainer tier

**Increase your income by 10% by claiming ownership of the Actor on Apify Store**. Youâ€™ll get insights into the performance of your commissions and weâ€™ll send the payouts directly to you. Apify customers will pay for the platform resources to run your software.

## Active developer tier

Maximize your income with the pay-per-event pricing model. Set your own prices and optimize your Actorâ€™s performance. The cost of computing resources is deducted from what customers pay for each run. You receive your earnings and commissions monthly.   
  
For active developers, we offer a competitive advantageâ€”either a significantly reduced Apify margin or discounted compute unit pricing.

[Monetize your code](/partners/actor-developers)

## Why join the Apify fair share program?

Get sponsored

Turn your open-source project into a product and start earning.

Monetize with minimal effort

Set your price, publish on Apify, and let us handle the rest.

Reach thousands

Share your work with a global audience and make an impact.

Earn passive income

Enjoy commissions with minimal effort while scaling your project.

## Get started now

Get rewarded for turning open-source projects into Actors.

[Join the program](https://apify.firstpromoter.com/signup/28997)

# Apify for nonprofits

We believe that online data can help your organization have more impact, so we're offering a substantial discount to nonprofits and NGOs.

Apply now

Supporting these amazing nonprofit organizations

[](/success-stories/fighting-child-traffickers-with-technology)[](https://blog.apify.com/apify-and-czechitas/)[](https://blog.apify.com/using-web-scraping-to-preserve-digital-memory-of-war-crimes-in-ukraine/)[](/success-stories/helping-the-planet-with-data)

## Start scraping right away

Find data for your nonprofit or NGO with 2,000+ ready-made tools (Actors) available on [Apify Store](https://apify.com/store). You can search for an Actor that scrapes specific website data needed for your [use case](https://apify.com/use-cases) or fine-tune [universal web scrapers](https://apify.com/scrapers/universal-web-scrapers) that require some coding knowledge.

### [Instagram Scraperapify/instagram-scraperScrape and download Instagram posts, profiles, places, hashtags, photos, and comments. Get data from Instagram using one or more Instagram URLs or search queries. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs or integrate with other tools.Apify78.7k4.3/5](/apify/instagram-scraper)### [Web Scraperapify/web-scraperCrawls arbitrary websites using the Chrome browser and extracts structured data from web pages using a provided JavaScript function. The Actor supports both recursive crawling and lists of URLs, and automatically manages concurrency for maximum performance.Apify77.6k4.5/5](/apify/web-scraper)### [Google Maps Scrapercompass/crawler-google-placesExtract data from thousands of Google Maps locations and businesses. Get Google Maps data including reviews, reviewer details, images, contact info, opening hours, location, prices & more. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs, or integrate with other tools.Compass87.6k4.5/5](/compass/crawler-google-places)### [TikTok Scraperclockworks/tiktok-scraperExtract data from TikTok videos, hashtags, and users. Use URLs or search queries to scrape TikTok profiles, hashtags, posts, URLs, shares, followers, hearts, names, video, and music-related data. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs or integrate with other tools.Clockworks22.2k4.5/5](/clockworks/tiktok-scraper)### [Social Media Sentiment Analysis Tooltri_angle/social-media-sentiment-analysis-toolAdd a profile name and find this social profile on Facebook, Instagram, and TikTok, scrape its recent posts and comments, and perform sentiment analysis for each comment. All in one go. Export results in JSON, CSV, HTML, use API, schedule runs, integrate with other tools.TriâŸangle5924.2/5](/tri_angle/social-media-sentiment-analysis-tool)### [Twitter Scraperquacker/twitter-scraperScrape tweets from any Twitter user profile. Top Twitter API alternative to scrape Twitter hashtags, threads, replies, followers, images, videos, statistics, and Twitter history. Export scraped data, run the scraper via API, schedule and monitor runs or integrate with other tools.Quacker31.6k4.3/5](/quacker/twitter-scraper)

[Browse 2,000+ ready-made scrapers](https://apify.com/store)

## Develop what you need yourself

Use your own code and run it on the Apify platform to automate your workflow in the cloud and [integrate it](https://apify.com/integrations) with other services. The [Apify Docs](https://docs.apify.com/) have everything you need to get started.

[Start with PythonScrape single page with provided URL with HTTPX and extract data from page's HTML with Beautiful Soup.](/templates/python-start)[Start with JavaScriptScrape single page with provided URL with Axios and extract data from page's HTML with Cheerio.](/templates/js-start)[Start with TypeScriptScrape single page with provided URL with Axios and extract data from page's HTML with Cheerio.](/templates/ts-start)

[View more web scraping templates](/templates)

## See how other organizations use Apify

Apify has been used to battle human trafficking, find missing children, help find sustainable policies, identify misleading pricing, track the spread of disease, and many other use cases that have improved the lives of ordinary people all over the world.

[HlÃ­daÄ shopÅ¯ monitors prices of online stores and provides consumers with tools to avoid misleading pricing strategies.](https://www.hlidacshopu.cz/)[Thorn scrapes data from multiple escort sites and identifies missing children that have become victims to human trafficking](/success-stories/fighting-child-traffickers-with-technology)[Czechitas is a Czech non-profit organization on a mission to promote and increase diversity in the IT industry.](/success-stories/women-it-opportunity)

[See all customer stories](/success-stories)

## How do I sign up for the discount?

1

### Fill out the form

First, create an Apify account with your organization email and then fill out the form below. Please note that discounts are only available for organizations that meet certain criteria.

2

### Wait for Apifyâ€™s response

Our team will review your application. Give us time for this step! If we find your use case suitable, we'll reach out to you. We might even jump on a call to make sure you have everything you need.

3

### Make the most of your discount!

Once we've decided on the terms of your platform usage, we'll modify your Apify account so that you can extract data at a reduced rate.

4

### Mention Apify on your website

We would be delighted if you would consider referencing Apify on your website, and in your research papers and online publications. This will help your colleagues and peers discover how web scraping can be used as a force for good.

Fill out the form

## Frequently asked questions

### Who is eligible? 

Any qualifying nonprofit, NGO, 501(c)(3) or equivalent that is registered within the operating country.

### Are there any restrictions on the type of organization that can apply for the discount?

While most nonprofits and NGOs are eligible, we reserve the right to reject any application.

### How long will I be able to use my discount?

You can enjoy the discount for 6 months, with the possibility of an extension to 12 months if you really need it. You can request an extension up to 1 month before expiry.

### What level of support will I recieve?

We love working with nonprofits and always try our best to offer them special care. While we aim to provide an extra support for all the nonprofits we work with, the level of assistance you can expect will ultimately depend on the plan you choose. You can find the details of our support options for each pricing plan on the [pricing page](https://apify.com/pricing).

### When will I know if the discount is approved? 

We typically reply within 5 business days.

### Are there any other requirements?

If your organization receives media coverage or publishes academic papers, you're obliged to mention Apify when referring to the method of gathering data.

## Why youâ€™ll love being an Apify affiliate

The Apify Affiliate Program gives you the chance to earn recurring commission on platform usage arising from any of these models.

[**Apify Store** Promote the largest web scraping marketplace with 3,000+ pre-built scrapers that can solve many use cases right out of the box and don't require any coding skills.](/store)[**Freelancers and Actor developers** Build solutions for your customers on Apify for a fee, or publish Actors on Apify Store and earn passive income. Plus collect recurring commission from subscriptions.](/partners/freelancers)[**Professional services** Refer customers that need custom web scraping solutions to us, and if the deal goes through, we will pay up to $2,500 per closed-won customer.](/professional-services)

## Who are we looking for?

The Apify Affiliate Program is very inclusive and welcomes everyone who understands the value of web data and automation. Whether you have an authoritative website, an established social media presence, or specialized skills in tech and data, we're looking for you!

Developers and freelancers

Web scraping and automation [freelancers](https://apify.com/partners/freelancers), [Paid Actor Developers](https://apify.com/partners/actor-developers), data scientists leveraging web scraping for data collection, and automation consultants implementing web scraping solutions

Educators and trainers

Online course creators, coding bootcamps, and business coaches or consultants covering web scraping, data, generative AI or LLMs

Digital agencies

Digital marketing, SEO, and web development agencies that understand value of web scraping for market research and solutions

Content creators

Tech bloggers, YouTubers and podcasters covering web scraping, automation, or AI topics

Industry influencers

Thought leaders, influencers, and data advocates focusing on web scraping, tech, or data acquisition

Communities and forums

Forum admins for tech communities or leaders of online groups with a focus on web scraping

## What's in it for you?

Combine with other programs

Affiliate program isn't the only way to make money on Apify. You can also generate passive income by [developing Paid Actors](https://apify.com/partners/actor-developers) or by building custom solutions as a [freelancer](https://apify.com/partners/freelancers).

The only platform with a free trial

Apify is the only platform that offers $5 free trial that renews each month. So users you refer to us are able to try tools before subscribing, which means better conversion rates. ðŸ˜‹

Painless billing

Get paid via a bank transfer or PayPal and receive your money within 30 days from your first referral. Track your referrals in real-time from a transparent dashboard.

No time limits on the commissions

Get 20% commission for every customer you bring in their first 3 months and then 30% commission in the following months for as long as they stay our customers.

No self-referrals & paid ads

Or paid advertising/PPC activities (such as Google Ads, Facebook Ads or Linkedin Ads)

Cookies

When you send users our way, cookies will be able to track them for the next 45 days

[See full terms](https://apify.com/partners/affiliate/terms)

## Become an Apify Affiliate in a few clicks

1

### Sign up

Create an account on our [FirstPromoter portal](https://apify.firstpromoter.com/). Youâ€™ll gain access to your referral links and promotional material you can use for your campaigns.

2

### Promote Apify

Share your links with your audience via social media, videos, blog posts, or any other organic channels. Use any of our marketing materials or request new ones. Think a discount coupon might help you bring more customers? Let us know and we will create one for your community.

3

### Get paid

Track your performance in real-time and request a payout on an irregular date. Plus, you'll pocket your commission even years later if the customer continues using Apify (up to $2,500 per customer).

## How much will you earn?

The amount you earn will vary based on the plan that you refer to users sent our way.

[See full pricing](/pricing)

## Weâ€™re the real deal

Our tools and services are trusted by developers and businesses all over the world. Don't take our word for it, check what our customers have to say about us and why Apify is the best web scraping and automation platform on the market.

## Frequently asked questions

### Can I advertise using a direct link?

Yes, after registration, you'll receive unique referral links that you can share with your audience. You can also customize these links to your liking.

### Can I refer enterprise customers that require custom solution?

Yes you can! We can pay up to $2,000 per closed-won customer + a recurring commission from the subscription. For these referrals, you can send introductions to [sales@apify.com](mailto:sales@apify.com) directly or refer them to our [Enterprise services](https://apify.com/custom-solutions).

### What is the commission payment period?

Commissions are paid out of subscriptions via PayPal or bank transfer at the beginning of each month. You'll need to fill in your information in First Promoter before we can send you your earnings.

### What is the minimum payout amount?

The minimum payout is $49, but we can make some exceptions. Please note that for any payout below $49 we will need you to send us an invoice.

### Can I receive my commission via PayPal?

Yes.

### How do I get my payout?

Youâ€™ll receive a regular email update with your accumulated earnings. When you are ready to withdaw your earnings, you can reply to that email and we will process your request. You can also exchange your earnings for Apify credits, in such case your earnings would be increased by another 15%, so for $100 in commission earnings you'd be able to get $115 in Apify credits.

### What's the commission cap per customer? 

You can earn up to $2,500 per each customer you refer to us. There is no time limit on the commission, so if you refer a customer that will take months or possibly years to reach this cap, you'd be getting the commission during this whole period as well.

### Can I advertise Apify on Google Search myself?

No, any advertising activities and/or promotions using Google Ads/Adwords, Facebook Ads, Instagram Ads, LinkedIn Ads or any similar online marketing tool that either uses a policy based on or derived from pay-per-click marketing tools, is strictly prohibited and can lead to the termination of your account. Also please note that from August 2023, all referrals via paid search campaigns are blocked automatically by the system and hence you won't even see these referrals on your dashboard.

### How much do your affiliate partners earn on average? 

Earnings among our affiliate partners can vary widely from a couple hundreds to thousands of dollars per month because it's really up to you and how actively you promote Apify. We set no upper earning limitsâ€”the sky's the limit! Well, almost: the maximum payout per customer is capped at $2,500. Beyond that, your earning potential is truly in your hands. The more you promote Apify, the more you stand to earn. It's that simple!

### What types of promotional materials are provided? 

You will get access to a full package of different banners, images, logos, badges and links that you can use in your campaigns. If there are more materials that might help you, just send us an email and we can discuss.

## Referring an enterprise customer?

Or perhaps you are a **top affiliate** and you're thinking of promoting Apify exclusively? Contact us at [partners@apify.com](mailto:partners@apify.com) to discuss a custom commission structure and support you might need.

[Contact us](mailto:partners@apify.com)

# Amazon Scraper

junglee/free-amazon-product-scraper

[Try for free](https://console.apify.com/actors/XVDTQc4a7MDTqSTMJ?addFromActorId=XVDTQc4a7MDTqSTMJ)

Pay $10.00 for 1,000 results

Gets you product data from Amazon. Unofficial API. Scrapes and downloads product information without using the Amazon API, including reviews, prices, descriptions, and ASIN.

## What is Free Amazon Product Scraper and how does it work?

Free Amazon Product Scraper is a web scraping tool that enables you to extract product data from Amazon by using Amazon's category URLs.

Simply insert the URL from Amazon in the input field and select the maximum number of items you want to scrape. Then download the data from the Dataset tab.

For an input example, check the [Input tab](https://apify.com/junglee/free-amazon-product-scraper/input-schema).

## 7 pages Amazon limitation

Amazon sometimes restricts search terms to a maximum of 7 pages, please validate the number of pages in the URL. To overcome this limit, try to use one of the regular categories and combine it with the search terms. E.g. instead of just searching for `Diamond rings`, find `Jewelry` or `Women's rings` category and combine them with the search term.

## How much will scraping with Free Amazon Product Scraper cost you?

When it comes to scraping, it can be challenging to estimate the resources needed to extract data as use cases may vary significantly. That's why the best course of action is to run a test scrape with a small sample of input data and limited output. Youâ€™ll get your price per scrape, which youâ€™ll then multiply by the number of scrapes you intend to do.

[Watch this video](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kOy8C6_5ZU4) for a few helpful tips. And don't forget that choosing a higher plan will save you money in the long run.

## Need to find product pairs between Amazon and another online shop?

Try our [AI Product Matcher](https://apify.com/equidem/ai-product-matcher). This AI model was created to compare items from different web stores, identifying exact matches and comparing real-time data obtained via web scraping. With the AI Product Matcher, you can use scraped product data to monitor product matches across the industry, implement dynamic pricing for your website, replace or complement manual mapping, and obtain realistic estimates against your competition for upcoming promo campaigns.

Most importantly, it is relatively easy to get started with (just follow [this Product Matcher guide](https://blog.apify.com/product-matching-ai-pricing-intelligence-web-scraping/)), and it can check thousands of pairs of products.

## Why scrape Amazon products?

Scraping Amazon products can help you to:

  * monitor the performance of categories and subcategories on Amazon so you can put the performance of your own products into context.
  * discover up-and-coming brands and products to benchmark your performance within its category based on views, conversions and reviews.
  * fine-tune your advertising and messaging.
